//The Inferno Demon is a mighty demon with full control over the power of fire. This monster took a shit load of time to create and perfect, I hope you like it.
//I recommend to use it only as a boss like monster as it is extremely powerful and can kill you really fast if you haven't mastered dodging. He can't hurt himself
//cause he uses a damage type and is resistant to his own damage type. He has about 5 attacks, one of which has about 20 different combinations.

ACTOR InfernoDemon 12345
{

ACTOR BombTrail
{
  Radius 8
  Height 8
  Scale 1.0
  RenderStyle Add
  Projectile
  -ACTIVATEPCROSS
  -ACTIVATEIMPACT
  +SPAWNSOUNDSOURCE
   States
   {
   Spawn:
      SBLL ABCDEFGHIJ 1 Bright
      Goto Death
   Death:
      SBLL A 1 Bright A_SetTranslucent(0.5)
	  SBLL B 1 Bright A_SetTranslucent(0.4)
	  SBLL C 1 Bright A_SetTranslucent(0.3)
	  SBLL D 1 Bright A_SetTranslucent(0.2)
	  SBLL E 1 Bright A_SetTranslucent(0.1)
      stop
   }
}

ACTOR FireBeam
{
Height 10
Radius 10
DamageType "Inferno"
Obituary "%o was sent to burn in the fires of hell for an eternity."
PROJECTILE
+DropOff
-NoGravity
+FloorHugger
+ExtremeDeath
+DontSplash
+Ripper
Speed 12
Scale 0.5
RENDERSTYLE Add
Alpha 0.75
Damage 5
ReactionTime 50
ACTIVESOUND "monster/firebeamstart"
states
{
Spawn:
HK04 A 0 
HK04 A 0 A_CountDown
HK04 A 0 A_LoopActiveSound
HK04 ABC 1 BRIGHT A_CustomMissile("BeamFire", 0, 0, 0, 4)
HK04 A 0 A_SeekerMissile (10, 25)
Goto Spawn+1
Death:
HK04 ABC 4
Stop
}
}
